	deploy_reserves_infantry = {

		icon = generic_nationalism

		available = {
			has_war = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = FRA
						original_tag = ITA
						original_tag = JAP
						original_tag = GER
						original_tag = SOV
						original_tag = ENG
						original_tag = USA
					}
				}
				has_manpower > 150999
			}
			else = {
				has_manpower > 150499
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SOV_has_civil_war_no_tt
				has_civil_war = no
				OR = {
					NOT = { tag = FRA }
					NOT = { has_war_with = VIC }
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { tag = ITA }
					NOT = { has_war_with = RIT }
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { tag = SOV }
					NOT = { has_war_with = STA }
				}
			}
			any_enemy_country = {
				OR = {
					ic_ratio = {
						tag = ROOT
						ratio > 0.25
					}
					is_major = yes
				}
			}
			NOT = { surrender_progress > 0.8 }
			num_of_controlled_states > 0
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = SOV
					is_ai = no
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = SOV_beaten_but_not_defeated }
				}
				has_completed_focus = SOV_emergency_powers
			}
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = reserves_finished_1 }
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = reserve_total_1
				has_country_flag = reserve_total_2
				has_country_flag = reserve_total_3
				has_country_flag = reserve_total_4
				has_country_flag = reserve_total_5
				has_country_flag = reserve_total_6
				has_country_flag = reserve_total_7
				has_country_flag = reserve_total_8
				has_country_flag = reserve_total_9
				has_country_flag = reserve_total_10
			}
		}

		cost = 5

		days_remove = 1

		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					is_ai = yes
				}
				add_manpower = -230000
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = FRA
						original_tag = ITA
						original_tag = JAP
						original_tag = GER
						original_tag = SOV
						original_tag = ENG
						original_tag = USA
					}
				}
				add_manpower = -151000
			}
			else = {
				add_manpower = -150500
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = reserve_total_1
				}
				clr_country_flag = reserve_total_1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = reserve_total_2
				}
				clr_country_flag = reserve_total_2
				set_country_flag = reserve_total_1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = reserve_total_3
				}

			if = {

	ENG_disband_the_home_guard = {
		icon = generic_political_discourse
		available = {
			original_tag = ENG
		}
		visible = {
			original_tag = ENG
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = home_guard_late_deployed
				has_country_flag = home_guard_deployed
			}
		}

		days_remove = 90
		is_good = yes
		cost = 50

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war = yes
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_home_guard_disbanded_tt
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Home Guard Unit"
				disband = yes
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Home Guard Unit Late"
				disband = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = ENG_home_guard_disbanded
			}
		}
